				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Fidelio, Op.72 (Beethoven, Ludwig van)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts [1st version]<br />2 acts [2nd/3rd versions]
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1804–05 [1st version], 1805 [2nd version], 1814 [3rd version]
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Operas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Operas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="21 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_voice&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the voice</a></span>; (Will have to check to see if that's an accurate description of what we have here. Probably not what Beethoven authorized...)

</th>
